(_( 2_CD )_) The_DT Agra_NNP Asylum_NNP was_VBD visited_VBN in_IN December_NNP ._.
I_PRP found_VBD it_PRP clean_JJ and_CC tidy_NN but_CC far_RB from_IN being_VBG so_RB pleasing_VBG to_TO the_DT eye_NN as_IN the_DT asylums_NNS at_IN Bareilly_NNP and_CC Benares_NNP ._.
